<script>
  function getEnviromentUrl() {
    let environmentUrl;
    const frontUrls = {
      qa: 'https://fastly-fwc26.qa.oledev.com',
      qam: 'https://fastly-fwc26.qam.oledev.com',
      uat: 'https://fifaworldcup26.pp-hospitality.fifa.com',
      prod: 'https://fifaworldcup26.hospitality.fifa.com',
      uatWF: 'https://webflow-fwc26.uat.oledev.com',
      prodWF: 'https://webflow-fwc26.fifaworldcup26.onlocationexp.com',
    };

    const currentUrl = window.parent.location.origin;
    switch (currentUrl) {
      case frontUrls.uatWF:
        environmentUrl = frontUrls.uat;
        break;
      case frontUrls.prodWF:
        environmentUrl = frontUrls.prod;
        break;
      default:
        environmentUrl = currentUrl;
        break;
    }
    return environmentUrl;
  }
</script>

<script>
  const getCurrentLang = () => {
    const langCode = document.documentElement.getAttribute('lang');
    if (langCode == 'es-MX') {
      return 'es';
    } else if (langCode == 'fr-CA') {
      return 'fr';
    }
    return 'en';
  };

</script>

<!-- Accordion Schema & Interaction Script -->
<script>
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
    // Define a unique key to store the initialization flag on the window object
    const ACCORDION_INIT_FLAG = "customAccordionInitialized";

    // Check if the script has already been initialized
    if (window[ACCORDION_INIT_FLAG]) {
        console.warn("Accordion script has already been initialized.");
        return;
    }

    // Function to initialize accordions and generate FAQ schema
    function initializeAccordions() {
        // Select all accordion groups
        const accordionGroups = document.querySelectorAll(
            '[cl-accordion="group"], [fs-accordion-element="group"], [cl-accordion="interlinking"]'
        );

        // If no groups are found, exit the script
        if (accordionGroups.length === 0) {
            console.info("No accordion groups found. Script will not run.");
            return;
        }

        // Array to hold FAQ items for the schema
        const faqItems = [];
        const topOffset = 200;

        function scrollToAccordionTrigger(group, clickedTrigger) {
            const groupTop =
                group.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.pageYOffset;
            const allTriggers = group.querySelectorAll(
                '[cl-accordion="trigger"], [fs-accordion-element="trigger"]'
            );

            let totalHeight = 0;
            for (let i = 0; i < allTriggers.length; i++) {
                const trigger = allTriggers[i];
                if (trigger === clickedTrigger) break;

                const triggerHeight = trigger.getBoundingClientRect().height;
                const triggerStyle = window.getComputedStyle(trigger);
                const marginBottom = parseFloat(triggerStyle.marginBottom);
                totalHeight += triggerHeight + marginBottom;
            }

            const scrollPosition = groupTop + totalHeight - topOffset;
            window.scrollTo({ top: scrollPosition, behavior: "smooth" });
        }

        accordionGroups.forEach((group) => {
            const interactionType = group.getAttribute(
                "cl-accordion-interaction"
            );
            const accordions = group.querySelectorAll('[cl-accordion="item"], [fs-accordion-element="accordion"]');

            accordions.forEach((accordion) => {
                const trigger = accordion.querySelector(
                    '[cl-accordion="trigger"], [fs-accordion-element="trigger"]'
                );
                const content = accordion.querySelector(
                    '[cl-accordion="content"], [fs-accordion-element="content"]'
                );

                if (trigger && content) {
                    trigger.setAttribute("aria-controls", content.id);
                    content.setAttribute("aria-labelledby", trigger.id);

                    const questionElement = trigger.querySelector(
                        '[cl-accordion="header-text"]'
                    );
                    const questionText = questionElement
                        ? questionElement.textContent.trim()
                        : "";

                    const answerElement = content.querySelector(
                        ".content-rich-text"
                    );
                    const answerText = answerElement
                        ? answerElement.innerHTML.trim()
                        : "";

                    if (questionText && answerText) {
                        faqItems.push({
                            "@type": "Question",
                            name: questionText,
                            acceptedAnswer: {
                                "@type": "Answer",
                                text: answerText,
                            },
                        });
                    }

                    if (interactionType === "true") {
                        trigger.addEventListener("click", () => {
                            const isExpanded =
                                trigger.getAttribute("aria-expanded") === "true";

                            scrollToAccordionTrigger(group, trigger);

                            if (isExpanded) return;

                            setTimeout(() => {
                                const updatedAccordions =
                                    group.querySelectorAll(
                                        '[cl-accordion="item"], [fs-accordion-element="accordion"]'
                                    );

                                updatedAccordions.forEach((otherAccordion) => {
                                    const otherTrigger =
                                        otherAccordion.querySelector(
                                            '[cl-accordion="trigger"], [fs-accordion-element="trigger"]'
                                        );
                                    if (
                                        otherTrigger !== trigger &&
                                        otherTrigger.getAttribute(
                                            "aria-expanded"
                                        ) === "true"
                                    ) {
                                        otherTrigger.click();
                                    }
                                });
                            }, 10);
                        });
                    } /*else if (interactionType === "false") {
                        trigger.addEventListener("click", () => {
                            scrollToAccordionTrigger(group, trigger);
                        });
                    } */
                } else {
                    console.warn(
                        "Accordion is missing either a trigger or content element:",
                        accordion
                    );
                }
            });
        });

        if (faqItems.length > 0) {
            const faqSchema = {
                "@context": "https://schema.org",
                "@type": "FAQPage",
                "name": "FIFA World Cup 2026 FAQ",
                mainEntity: faqItems,
            };

            const script = document.createElement("script");
            script.type = "application/ld+json";
            script.text = JSON.stringify(faqSchema, null, 2);
            document.head.appendChild(script);

            console.log("FAQ Schema has been successfully generated.");
        } else {
            console.warn("No valid FAQ items found to generate schema.");
        }

        window[ACCORDION_INIT_FLAG] = true;
        console.log("Accordion script initialized.");
    }

    initializeAccordions();
});
</script>

<!-- Accessible Accordion Script -->
<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
    const accordionState = new Map(); // Store open accordion states per group

    // Function to open an accordion
    const openAccordion = (button, content) => {
        button.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'true');
        content.style.display = 'block';
        setTimeout(() => content.style.maxHeight = content.scrollHeight + 'px', 0);

        // Add 'is-active' class to the accordion header
        const header = button.closest('[cl-accordion="trigger"]');
        if (header) header.classList.add('is-active');
    };

    // Function to close an accordion
    const closeAccordion = (button, content) => {
        button.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
        content.style.maxHeight = '0';
        setTimeout(() => content.style.display = 'none', 350);

        // Remove 'is-active' class from the accordion header
        const header = button.closest('[cl-accordion="trigger"]');
        if (header) header.classList.remove('is-active');
    };

    // Function to restore previously open accordions
    const restoreAccordionState = (group) => {
        const savedButtons = accordionState.get(group) || new Set();
        savedButtons.forEach(buttonId => {
            const button = group.querySelector(`#${buttonId}`);
            const content = group.querySelector(`[cl-accordion="content"][aria-labelledby="${buttonId}"]`);
            if (button && content) openAccordion(button, content);
        });
    };

    // Function to initialize accordions
    const initAccordion = (group) => {
        const buttons = group.querySelectorAll('[cl-accordion="trigger"]');
        const singleAccordion = group.getAttribute('cl-accordion-single') === 'true';
        const shouldOpenFirst = group.getAttribute('cl-accordion-initial') !== 'false'; // Default to true
        const isInterlinking = group.getAttribute('cl-accordion') === 'interlinking';

        // Open the first accordion only if it's not an "interlinking" group
        if (!isInterlinking && shouldOpenFirst && !accordionState.has(group)) {
            const firstButton = buttons[0];
            if (firstButton) {
                const firstContent = group.querySelector(`[cl-accordion="content"][aria-labelledby="${firstButton.id}"]`);
                if (firstButton && firstContent) {
                    openAccordion(firstButton, firstContent);
                    accordionState.set(group, new Set([firstButton.id])); // Save state
                }
            }
        }

        buttons.forEach(button => {
            button.addEventListener('click', function () {
                const content = group.querySelector(`[cl-accordion="content"][aria-labelledby="${button.id}"]`);
                const isExpanded = button.getAttribute('aria-expanded') === 'true';

                let openAccordions = accordionState.get(group) || new Set();

                // Close all other accordions if single mode is enabled
                if (singleAccordion) {
                    buttons.forEach(otherButton => {
                        if (otherButton !== button) {
                            const otherContent = group.querySelector(`[cl-accordion="content"][aria-labelledby="${otherButton.id}"]`);
                            if (otherButton && otherContent) {
                                closeAccordion(otherButton, otherContent);
                                openAccordions.delete(otherButton.id);
                            }
                        }
                    });
                }

                // Toggle current accordion
                if (isExpanded) {
                    closeAccordion(button, content);
                    openAccordions.delete(button.id);
                } else {
                    openAccordion(button, content);
                    openAccordions.add(button.id);
                }

                accordionState.set(group, openAccordions);
            });

            button.addEventListener('keydown', function (e) {
                if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    button.click();
                }
            });
        });
    };

    // Initialize all accordion groups dynamically
    const accordionGroups = document.querySelectorAll('[cl-accordion^="group"]');
    accordionGroups.forEach(group => initAccordion(group));

    // Handle tab switching and restore accordions
    const tabLinks = document.querySelectorAll('[cl-tabs-link]');
    tabLinks.forEach(tabLink => {
        tabLink.addEventListener('click', function () {
            const panelId = tabLink.getAttribute('aria-controls');
            const targetTab = document.getElementById(panelId);

            setTimeout(() => {
                const targetAccordionGroup = targetTab.querySelector('[cl-accordion^="group"]');
                if (targetAccordionGroup) restoreAccordionState(targetAccordionGroup);
            }, 10);
        });
    });
});
</script>


<!-- Accesible Tabs Script -->
<script>
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
  document.querySelectorAll('[cl-tabs-wrapper]').forEach(tabWrapper => {
    const tabs = tabWrapper.querySelectorAll('[cl-tabs-link]');
    const panels = tabWrapper.querySelectorAll('[role="tabpanel"]');

    function activateTab(tab) {
      const panelId = tab.getAttribute("aria-controls");
      const activePanel = tabWrapper.querySelector(`#${panelId}`);
      const currentPanel = tabWrapper.querySelector('[role="tabpanel"].active');

      if (currentPanel === activePanel) return; // Prevent reactivating the same tab

      // Update aria-selected for tabs within this wrapper
      tabs.forEach(t => t.setAttribute("aria-selected", "false"));
      tab.setAttribute("aria-selected", "true");

      // Fade out the current panel before switching
      if (currentPanel) {
        currentPanel.style.opacity = "0";
        currentPanel.style.pointerEvents = "none";

        setTimeout(() => {
          currentPanel.classList.remove('active'); // Remove active only after fade-out
          activePanel.classList.add('active');

          // Small delay before fading in the new panel
          setTimeout(() => {
            activePanel.style.opacity = "1";
            activePanel.style.pointerEvents = "all";
          }, 50);
        }, 300);
      } else {
        // If no panel was previously active, just show the new one
        activePanel.classList.add('active');
        setTimeout(() => {
          activePanel.style.opacity = "1";
          activePanel.style.pointerEvents = "all";
        }, 50);
      }
    }

    function handleKeydown(e, tab) {
      if (e.key === "ArrowUp" || e.key === "ArrowDown") {
        e.preventDefault();
        const newTab = e.key === "ArrowDown"
          ? tab.nextElementSibling || tabs[0]
          : tab.previousElementSibling || tabs[tabs.length - 1];

        newTab.focus();
        activateTab(newTab);
      }
    }

    tabs.forEach(tab => {
      tab.addEventListener("click", () => activateTab(tab));
      tab.addEventListener("keydown", (e) => handleKeydown(e, tab));
    });

    activateTab(tabs[0]); // Set initial active tab for each group
  });
});
</script>

<!-- Replace Attribute Script -->
<script>
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
    document.querySelectorAll('[cl-accordion^="group"]').forEach(group => {
      const groupNumber = group.getAttribute('cl-accordion').split('-')[1] || 1;

      group.querySelectorAll('[cl-accordion="trigger"]').forEach((trigger, index) => {
        const triggerId = `accordion-trigger-${index + 1}-${groupNumber}`;
        const contentId = `accordion-content-${index + 1}-${groupNumber}`;
        
        trigger.id = triggerId;
        trigger.setAttribute('aria-controls', contentId);

        group.querySelectorAll('[cl-accordion="content"]')[index].id = contentId;
        group.querySelectorAll('[cl-accordion="content"]')[index].setAttribute('aria-labelledby', triggerId);
      });
    });
  });

      } else if (mediaType === "custom-video-embed") {
        component.querySelectorAll(":scope .media_video, :scope .media_image-wrapper").forEach(el => el.remove());
      }
    });
  });

<script>
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
  function isResponsive() {
    return window.innerWidth <= 991; // Adjust breakpoint as needed
  }

  document.querySelectorAll(".nav_menu-dropdown").forEach(dropdown => {
    const toggle = dropdown.querySelector("[cl-nav-toggle]");
    const content = dropdown.querySelector("[cl-nav-content]");
    if (!toggle || !content) return;

    toggle.addEventListener("click", function (event) {
      event.stopPropagation();
      const isOpen = toggle.classList.contains("open");

      document.querySelectorAll(".nav_menu-dropdown").forEach(otherDropdown => {
        if (otherDropdown !== dropdown) {
          const otherToggle = otherDropdown.querySelector("[cl-nav-toggle]");
          const otherContent = otherDropdown.querySelector("[cl-nav-content]");
          if (otherToggle && otherContent) {
            otherToggle.classList.remove("open");
            otherContent.classList.remove("open");
            otherContent.style.maxHeight = null;
            otherToggle.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "false");
          }
        }
      });

      toggle.classList.toggle("open", !isOpen);
      content.classList.toggle("open", !isOpen);
      toggle.setAttribute("aria-expanded", !isOpen);

      if (isResponsive()) {
        if (!isOpen) {
          content.style.maxHeight = content.scrollHeight + "px";
        } else {
          content.style.maxHeight = null;
        }
      }
    });
  });

  document.addEventListener("click", function (event) {
    document.querySelectorAll(".nav_menu-dropdown").forEach(dropdown => {
      const toggle = dropdown.querySelector("[cl-nav-toggle]");
      const content = dropdown.querySelector("[cl-nav-content]");
      if (!toggle || !content) return;

      if (!dropdown.contains(event.target)) {
        toggle.classList.remove("open");
        content.classList.remove("open");
        content.style.maxHeight = null;
        toggle.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "false");
      }
    });
  });

  window.addEventListener("resize", function () {
    if (!isResponsive()) {
      document.querySelectorAll(".nav_menu-dropdown [cl-nav-content]").forEach(content => {
        content.style.maxHeight = null; // Reset max-height on larger screens
      });
    }
  });
});
</script>

<script>
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
  let navMenu = document.querySelector(".nav_menu");

  if (!navMenu) return;

  let observer = new MutationObserver(() => {
    navMenu.scrollTop = 0;
  });

  observer.observe(navMenu, { attributes: true, childList: true, subtree: true });

  document.querySelectorAll(".nav_menu-dropdown").forEach((dropdown) => {
    dropdown.addEventListener("click", function () {
      setTimeout(() => {
        navMenu.scrollTop = 0;
      }, 10); // Small delay to ensure content expands first
    });
  });
});

</script>

<!-- Calculate First Section Padding based on Nav Height -->
<script>
  document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
    function adjustPaddingTop() {
      var navWrapper = document.querySelector(".nav_component");
      var firstSection = document.querySelector(".main-wrapper > header");
      var allSections = document.querySelectorAll(".main-wrapper section");

      if (navWrapper && firstSection) {
        firstSection.style.transition = "padding-top 0.35s ease-in-out";
        firstSection.style.paddingTop = navWrapper.offsetHeight + "px";

        // Delay visibility to prevent transition effect on page load
        setTimeout(() => {
          allSections.forEach(section => {
            section.style.visibility = "visible";
            firstSection.style.visibility = "visible";
          });
        }, 350);
      }
    }

    setTimeout(adjustPaddingTop, 50); // Slight delay on initial load
    window.addEventListener("resize", adjustPaddingTop);

    var bannerCloseButton = document.querySelector("[banner-close-button]");
    if (bannerCloseButton) {
      bannerCloseButton.addEventListener("click", function () {
        adjustPaddingTop(); // No delay here
      });
    }

    var observer = new MutationObserver(adjustPaddingTop);
    var navWrapper = document.querySelector(".nav_component");
    if (navWrapper) {

    }
  });

wf.ready(() => {
// Function to opt in or out based on consent preferences
const handleWebflowAnalyticsConsent = () => {
   try {
      // Logic to check consent groups from the OneTrust cookie
      const otCookieKey = 'OptanonConsent=';
      const otCookie = document.cookie.split('; ').find(row => row.startsWith(otCookieKey));
      if (!otCookie) {
      throw new Error('OneTrust cookie not found.');
      }
      const otGroupsKey = 'groups=';
      const otGroups = decodeURIComponent(otCookie.split('&').find(row => row.startsWith(otGroupsKey)).split('=')[1]);
      // OneTrust groups: 1 = necessary, 2 = performance, 3 = functional, 4 = targeting
      const OT_FUNCTIONAL_CONSENT = '3:1'; // Ensure this matches your expected consent group
      // Check for functional cookies group
      const hasOptedIn = otGroups.indexOf(OT_FUNCTIONAL_CONSENT) !== -1;
      // Adjust Webflow Analytics opt-in/out based on consent
      if (hasOptedIn) {
      wf.allowUserTracking();
      } else {
      wf.denyUserTracking();
      }
   } catch (e) {
      console.error('Error handling OneTrust consent:', e);
   }
};
// Set up the OneTrust consent change listener to check when preferences change
if (typeof OneTrust !== 'undefined' && OneTrust.OnConsentChanged) {
   OneTrust.OnConsentChanged(() => {
      handleWebflowAnalyticsConsent();
   });
}
// Initial check when the page loads
handleWebflowAnalyticsConsent();
});

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
  const buttons = document.querySelectorAll('[data-country]');
  const pathParts = window.location.pathname.split('/').filter(Boolean);

  // pathParts = ['us', 'en'] example
  const currentLang = pathParts[1] || 'en';

  buttons.forEach(btn => {
    btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
      const newCountry = btn.dataset.country;
      const newUrl = `${window.location.origin}/${newCountry}/${currentLang}`;
      window.location.href = newUrl;
    });
  });
});
</script>

<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
  const popup = document.getElementById('country-popup');
  const changeBtn = document.getElementById('change-country');
  const buttons = document.querySelectorAll('.country-btn');

  // Get language from html tag
  let currentLang = document.documentElement.lang || 'en';

  // Check localStorage
  let selectedCountry = localStorage.getItem('selectedCountry');

  function showPopup() { popup.style.display = 'flex'; }
  function hidePopup() { popup.style.display = 'none'; }

  if (!selectedCountry) {
    showPopup();
    localStorage.setItem('selectedCountry', 'true');
  }

  buttons.forEach(btn => {
    btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
      const newCountry = btn.dataset.country;
      localStorage.setItem('selectedCountry', newCountry);
      hidePopup();

      // Redirect in format /country/lang
      const newUrl = `${window.location.origin}/${newCountry}/${currentLang}`;
      window.location.href = newUrl;
    });
  });

  changeBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
    showPopup();
  });
});
</script></div><div class="login-script w-embed w-script"><script>

        }

        const setEnvironment = () => {
            for (let environment in frontUrls) {
                if (frontUrls[environment] == window.parent.location.origin) {
                    currentEnvironment = environment;
                    return;
                }
            }

            currentEnvironment = 'prod';
        }

        const getCurrentCountry = () => {
            let countryCode = 'us';
            const firstPath = window.location.pathname.split('/')[1];
            if (firstPath == 'us' || firstPath == 'mx' || firstPath == 'ca') {
                countryCode = firstPath;
            }

            return countryCode;
        }

        const getCurrentLanguage = () => {
            const webflowLang = document.documentElement.lang;
            switch (webflowLang) {
                case 'en-US': return 'en';
                case 'es-MX': return 'es';
                case 'fr-CA': return 'fr';
                default: return 'en';
            }
        }

        const setMyAccountURL = (webflowLang, myAccountButton) => {
            const lang = getCurrentLanguage();
            const countryCode = getCurrentCountry();
            myAccountButton.href = `${secutixCountryUrls[currentEnvironment][countryCode]}/account?lang=${lang}`
        }

        const getCookie = (name) => {
            return document.cookie
                .split(";")
                .map(c => c.trim())
                .find(c => c.startsWith(name + "="))
                ?.split("=")[1] || null;
        }

        const debounce = (fn, delay = 150) => {
            let timeout;

            return () => {
                clearTimeout(timeout);
                timeout = setTimeout(fn, delay);
            };
        }

        const setValueIfElementExist = (element, value) => {
            if (!element) return;
            element.style.display = value;
        }

        const showHideMyAccountButton = () => {
            const loginButton = document.getElementById('login-header-label');
            const myAccountButton = document.getElementById('my-account-header');
            const loginButtonMobile = document.getElementById('login-header-label-mobile');
            const myAccountButtonMobile = document.getElementById('my-account-header-mobile');
            const accessToken = getCookie("access_token");

            loginButton.href = authUrls[currentEnvironment];
            loginButtonMobile.href = authUrls[currentEnvironment];
            if (accessToken) {
                setValueIfElementExist(loginButton, 'none');
                setValueIfElementExist(loginButtonMobile, 'none');
                setValueIfElementExist(myAccountButton, 'block');
                setValueIfElementExist(myAccountButtonMobile, 'block');
                setMyAccountURL(document.documentElement.lang, myAccountButton);
                setMyAccountURL(document.documentElement.lang, myAccountButtonMobile);
            } else {
                setValueIfElementExist(loginButton, 'block');
                setValueIfElementExist(loginButtonMobile, 'block');
                setValueIfElementExist(myAccountButton, 'none');
                setValueIfElementExist(myAccountButtonMobile, 'none');
            }

            if (window.innerWidth <= 990) {
                setValueIfElementExist(loginButton, 'none');
                setValueIfElementExist(myAccountButton, 'none');
            } else {
                setValueIfElementExist(loginButtonMobile, 'none');
                setValueIfElementExist(myAccountButtonMobile, 'none');
            }
        }

        setEnvironment();
        showHideMyAccountButton();
        window.addEventListener('resize', debounce(showHideMyAccountButton));
    })();

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {

  function initMobileTabs() {
    if (window.innerWidth > 767) return;

    var layout = document.querySelector('.header-selection_layout');
    var items = document.querySelectorAll('.header-selection_item');

    if (!layout || !items.length) return;

    // Створюємо окремий контейнер для активного dropdown (рядок 2)
    var dropdownRow = document.querySelector('.header-selection_active-dropdown');
    if (!dropdownRow) {
      dropdownRow = document.createElement('div');
      dropdownRow.classList.add('header-selection_active-dropdown');
      layout.appendChild(dropdownRow);
    }

    // Створюємо рядок для табів (рядок 1) якщо ще немає
    var tabsRow = document.querySelector('.header-selection_tabs-row');
    if (!tabsRow) {
      tabsRow = document.createElement('div');
      tabsRow.classList.add('header-selection_tabs-row');
      layout.insertBefore(tabsRow, layout.firstChild);
    }

    // Переміщуємо кожен item у рядок табів
    // і клонуємо dropdown окремо
    items.forEach(function (item) {
      // Виймаємо dropdown з item і зберігаємо як data
      var dropdown = item.querySelector('.header-selection_dropdown');
      if (dropdown && !item._mobileDropdown) {
        item._mobileDropdown = dropdown;
      }

      // Переміщуємо item у tabsRow якщо ще не там
      if (item.parentNode !== tabsRow) {
        tabsRow.appendChild(item);
      }

      item.addEventListener('click', function () {
        // Деактивуємо всі
        items.forEach(function (i) {
          i.classList.remove('is-active');
        });

        // Активуємо поточний
        item.classList.add('is-active');

        // Показуємо dropdown цього таба в рядку 2
        dropdownRow.innerHTML = '';
        if (item._mobileDropdown) {
          dropdownRow.appendChild(item._mobileDropdown);
        }
      });
    });

    // Активуємо перший таб за замовчуванням
    if (items[0]) {
      items[0].click();
    }
  }

  initMobileTabs();

  var resizeTimer;
  window.addEventListener('resize', function () {
    clearTimeout(resizeTimer);
    resizeTimer = setTimeout(initMobileTabs, 200);
  });

});
</script></div></div></div><div class="spacer-large"></div><div class="button-group is-position-center"><a class="button w-inline-block is-secondary is-alternate" data-wf-component-context="%5B%7B%22componentId%22%3A%22f607b846-9562-a410-d8b4-5c6efbf098a4%22%2C%22instanceId%22%3A%22b0710f2f-06db-a231-4feb-93677f81a203%22%7D%5D" data-wf-element-id="f607b846-9562-a410-d8b4-5c6efbf098a4" href="/us/en/choose-matches?src=home_hero_browse_matches" data-button="" data-button-size="" id="browse-all-matches" data-wf-native-id-path="b0710f2f-06db-a231-4feb-93677f81a203:f607b846-9562-a410-d8b4-5c6efbf098a4" data-wf-ao-click-engagement-tracking="true" data-id=""><div class="button_text">Browse All Matches</div></a></div><div class="hero-tabs_wrapper"><div class="spacer-xlarge"></div><div class="heading-style-h7 text-color-default-tertiary text-align-left">Browse</div><div class="tabs_nav-wrapper"><div class="locations-tabs_nav is-animate"><a data-tab="venues" data-wf-native-id-path="b0710f2f-06db-a231-4feb-93677f81a20b" data-wf-ao-click-engagement-tracking="true" data-wf-element-id="b0710f2f-06db-a231-4feb-93677f81a20b" href="#" class="locations-tabs_btn is-active">Host City</a><a data-tab="countries" data-wf-native-id-path="b0710f2f-06db-a231-4feb-93677f81a20d" data-wf-ao-click-engagement-tracking="true" data-wf-element-id="b0710f2f-06db-a231-4feb-93677f81a20d" href="#" class="locations-tabs_btn">Team</a></div></div><div id="venues" class="locations-tab_pane is-active"><div class="venues-slider_component"><div class="venues-slider_btns"><div class="venues-slider_btn_element is-prev"><div class="slider_btn_icon w-embed"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none">

    // Remove Aria Labels from the slider as they are not needed and can cause issues with screen readers
    (() => {
        const rolesFixex = {
            list: {
                requiredChildren: ['listitem'],
                fix: (el) => {
                    const children = Array.from(el.children);
                    let hasValid = children.some(child => child.getAttribute('role') === 'listitem');
                    if (!hasValid) {
                        children.forEach(child => {
                            if (!child.getAttribute('role')) {
                                child.setAttribute('role', 'listitem');
                            }
                        });

                        hasValid = children.some(child => child.getAttribute('role') === 'listitem');
                    }

                    return hasValid;
                }
            }
        };

        const cleanRoles = () => {
            Object.keys(rolesFixex).forEach(role => {
                document.querySelectorAll(`[role="${role}"]`).forEach(el => {
                    const config = rolesFixex[role];
                    const isValid = config.fix(el);
                    if (!isValid) {
                        el.removeAttribute('role');
                    }
                });
            });

            document.querySelectorAll('[role="group"]').forEach(el => {
                const parent = el.parentElement;
                if (parent?.getAttribute('role') === 'list') {
                    el.removeAttribute('role');
                }
            });
        };

        cleanRoles();

        const observer = new MutationObserver(cleanRoles);
        observer.observe(document.body, {
            childList: true,
            subtree: true
        });
    })();
</script></div></div></div><div class="w-embed w-script"><style>

<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
  const nav   = document.querySelector('.locations-tabs_nav');
  if (!nav) return;

  const btns  = [...nav.querySelectorAll('[data-tab]')];
  const panes = [...document.querySelectorAll('.locations-tab_pane')];
  const indicator = nav.querySelector('.tab-indicator');

  // utilities
  const byKey = (key) => btns.findIndex(b => b.dataset.tab === key);

  function updateIndicator() {
    const active = nav.querySelector('.locations-tabs_btn.is-active');
    if (!active || !indicator) return;

    const navRect = nav.getBoundingClientRect();
    const btnRect = active.getBoundingClientRect();
    const left = btnRect.left - navRect.left + nav.scrollLeft;

    indicator.style.width = `${btnRect.width}px`;
    indicator.style.transform = `translateX(${left}px)`;
  }

  function setActiveByKey(key, syncHash=false) {
    const idx = byKey(key);
    if (idx === -1) return;

    btns.forEach((b,i) => b.classList.toggle('is-active', i===idx));
    panes.forEach(p => p.classList.toggle('is-active', p.id === key));
    
    if (syncHash) history.replaceState(null, '', '#'+key);
    updateIndicator();
    
    //update all Swiper after switching tabs
    document.querySelectorAll('.swiper').forEach(sw => {
    if (sw.swiper) {
      sw.swiper.update();       // updates sizes
      sw.swiper.slideTo(0, 0); // returns to the first slide without animation
    }
  });
  }

  // button clicks
  btns.forEach(b => {
    b.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
      e.preventDefault();
      setActiveByKey(b.dataset.tab, true);
    });
  });

  // clicks on .tab_link (data-tab | data-target | href="#id")
  document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
    const link = e.target.closest('.tab_link');
    if (!link) return;
    let key = link.dataset.tab
           || link.dataset.target
           || (link.getAttribute('href') || '').replace(/^.*#/, '');
    if (!key) return;

    if (byKey(key) !== -1) {
      e.preventDefault();
      setActiveByKey(key, true);
      // On mobile — just scroll so that the active one is visible (without the “drum”)
      const activeBtn = btns.find(b => b.dataset.tab === key);
      if (activeBtn) {
        const pad = 16;
        const left = activeBtn.offsetLeft - pad;
        nav.scrollTo({ left, behavior: 'smooth' });
      }
    }
  });

  // keys (left/right + Home/End)
  nav.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
    const keys = ['ArrowLeft','ArrowRight','Home','End'];
    if (!keys.includes(e.key)) return;
    e.preventDefault();
    let idx = btns.findIndex(b => b.classList.contains('is-active'));
    if (e.key === 'ArrowRight') idx = Math.min(idx+1, btns.length-1);
    if (e.key === 'ArrowLeft')  idx = Math.max(idx-1, 0);
    if (e.key === 'Home')       idx = 0;
    if (e.key === 'End')        idx = btns.length-1;

    setActiveByKey(btns[idx].dataset.tab, true);
    btns[idx].focus();
    // easy autoscroll only when really needed (mobile/narrower views)
    const pad = 16;
    const left = btns[idx].offsetLeft - pad;
    nav.scrollTo({ left, behavior: 'smooth' });
  });

  // initial state
  const hash = location.hash?.slice(1);
  const startKey = btns.some(b => b.dataset.tab === hash) ? hash : btns[0]?.dataset.tab;
  if (startKey) setActiveByKey(startKey, false);

  // if fonts/level are loaded later — update the indicator
  window.addEventListener('load', updateIndicator);
  window.addEventListener('resize', updateIndicator);
});

</script>

<script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/gsap/3.12.5/gsap.min.js"></script>

<script>
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", () => {
  const images = document.querySelectorAll(".home-banner_image");
  const banner = document.querySelector(".home-banner_section");

  const bannerRect = banner.getBoundingClientRect();
  const finalPositions = [];

  images.forEach((img) => {
    const rect = img.getBoundingClientRect();
    const parentRect = banner.getBoundingClientRect();
    const xFinal = rect.left - parentRect.left;
    const yFinal = rect.top - parentRect.top;
    finalPositions.push({ x: xFinal, y: yFinal });
  });

  // Setting starting positions
  images.forEach((img, i) => {
    const rect = img.getBoundingClientRect();
    const pos = finalPositions[i];
    let xStart = pos.x;
    let yStart = pos.y;

    switch (i) {
      case 0: // top-left
        xStart += rect.width * 0.25;
        yStart += rect.height * 0.25;
        break;
      case 1: // top-right
        xStart -= rect.width * 0.25;
        yStart += rect.height * 0.25;
        break;
      case 2: // bottom-left
        xStart += rect.width * 0.25;
        yStart -= rect.height * 0.25;
        break;
      case 3: // bottom-right
        xStart -= rect.width * 0.25;
        yStart -= rect.height * 0.25;
        break;
    }

    // Starting parameters via GSAP
    let startOpacity = 0;

    // For top left on tablet/mobile opacity = 0.4
    if (img.classList.contains("top-left") && window.innerWidth <= 1200) {
      startOpacity = 0.4;
    }

    // For lower images on tablet/mobile, hide
    if ((img.classList.contains("bottom-left") || img.classList.contains("bottom-right")) && window.innerWidth <= 1200) {
      startOpacity = 0;
      gsap.set(img, { display: "none" });
    }

    gsap.set(img, {
      x: xStart - pos.x,
      y: yStart - pos.y,
      scale: 0.7,
      opacity: startOpacity,
    });
  });

  // Animation to the final positions
  const tl = gsap.timeline({ defaults: { ease: "power2.out" } });

  images.forEach((img, i) => {
    // If the image is hidden, skip the animation
    if ((img.classList.contains("bottom-left") || img.classList.contains("bottom-right")) && window.innerWidth <= 1200) return;

    let targetOpacity = 1;

    // Top left on tablet/mobile 0.4
    if (img.classList.contains("top-left") && window.innerWidth <= 1200) {
      targetOpacity = 0.4;
    }

    tl.to(
      img,
      {
        x: 0,
        y: 0,
        scale: 1,
        opacity: targetOpacity,
        duration: 1,
      },
      i * 0.2
    );
  });
});
</script></div></div></div><div class="section_home-info-block"><div class="section-spacer-xsmall"></div><div class="padding-global"><div class="container-medium"><div class="home_info-banners"><a       slideDuplicateActiveClass: "is-active",

        forceToAxis: true,
      },

        enabled: true,
        onlyInViewport: true,
      },

    });
  });
});

        enabled: true,
        onlyInViewport: true,
      },
      navigation: {
        nextEl: component.querySelector(".r32-slider_btn_element.is-next"),
        prevEl: component.querySelector(".r32-slider_btn_element.is-prev"),
      },
      pagination: {
        el: component.querySelector(".r32-slider_bullet_wrap"),
        bulletActiveClass: "is-active",
        bulletClass: "r32-slider_bullet_item",
        bulletElement: "button",
        clickable: true,
      },
      scrollbar: {
        el: component.querySelector(".r32-slider_draggable_wrap"),
        draggable: true,
        dragClass: "r32-slider_draggable_handle",
        snapOnRelease: true,
      },
    });
  });
});
</script>


<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
  const nav   = document.querySelector('.tabs_nav');
  if (!nav) return;

  const btns  = [...nav.querySelectorAll('[data-tab]')];
  const panes = [...document.querySelectorAll('.tab_pane')];
  const indicator = nav.querySelector('.tab-indicator');

  // utilities
  const byKey = (key) => btns.findIndex(b => b.dataset.tab === key);

  function updateIndicator() {
    const active = nav.querySelector('.tabs_btn.is-active');
    if (!active || !indicator) return;

    const navRect = nav.getBoundingClientRect();
    const btnRect = active.getBoundingClientRect();
    const left = btnRect.left - navRect.left + nav.scrollLeft;

    indicator.style.width = `${btnRect.width}px`;
    indicator.style.transform = `translateX(${left}px)`;
  }

  function setActiveByKey(key, syncHash=false) {
    const idx = byKey(key);
    if (idx === -1) return;

    btns.forEach((b,i) => b.classList.toggle('is-active', i===idx));
    panes.forEach(p => p.classList.toggle('is-active', p.id === key));
    
    if (syncHash) history.replaceState(null, '', '#'+key);
    updateIndicator();
    
    //update all Swiper after switching tabs
    document.querySelectorAll('.swiper').forEach(sw => {
    if (sw.swiper) {
      sw.swiper.update();       // updates sizes
      sw.swiper.slideTo(0, 0);  // returns to the first slide without animation
    }
  });
  }

  // button clicks
  btns.forEach(b => {
    b.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
      e.preventDefault();
      setActiveByKey(b.dataset.tab, true);
    });
  });

  // clicks on .tab_link (data-tab | data-target | href="#id")
  document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
    const link = e.target.closest('.tab_link');
    if (!link) return;
    let key = link.dataset.tab
           || link.dataset.target
           || (link.getAttribute('href') || '').replace(/^.*#/, '');
    if (!key) return;

    if (byKey(key) !== -1) {
      e.preventDefault();
      setActiveByKey(key, true);
      // On mobile — just scroll so that the active one is visible (without the “drum”)
      const activeBtn = btns.find(b => b.dataset.tab === key);
      if (activeBtn) {
        const pad = 16;
        const left = activeBtn.offsetLeft - pad;
        nav.scrollTo({ left, behavior: 'smooth' });
      }
    }
  });

  // keys (left/right + Home/End)
  nav.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
    const keys = ['ArrowLeft','ArrowRight','Home','End'];
    if (!keys.includes(e.key)) return;
    e.preventDefault();
    let idx = btns.findIndex(b => b.classList.contains('is-active'));
    if (e.key === 'ArrowRight') idx = Math.min(idx+1, btns.length-1);
    if (e.key === 'ArrowLeft')  idx = Math.max(idx-1, 0);
    if (e.key === 'Home')       idx = 0;
    if (e.key === 'End')        idx = btns.length-1;

    setActiveByKey(btns[idx].dataset.tab, true);
    btns[idx].focus();
    // easy autoscroll only when really needed (mobile/narrower views)
    const pad = 16;
    const left = btns[idx].offsetLeft - pad;
    nav.scrollTo({ left, behavior: 'smooth' });
  });

  // initial state
  const hash = location.hash?.slice(1);
  const startKey = btns.some(b => b.dataset.tab === hash) ? hash : btns[0]?.dataset.tab;
  if (startKey) setActiveByKey(startKey, false);

  // if fonts/level are loaded later — update the indicator
  window.addEventListener('load', updateIndicator);
  window.addEventListener('resize', updateIndicator);
});

</script>

<script>
  document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", () => {
    const blocks = document.querySelectorAll('.lounge-access_block');
    let current = 0;
    let interval;

    function activateBlock(index) {
      blocks.forEach((block, i) => {
        block.classList.remove('is-active');

        const desc = block.querySelector('.lounge-access_progress-decription');
        const title = block.querySelector('.lounge-access_progress-title');
        const fill = block.querySelector('.block-progress-fill');

        // Hide description
        if (desc) {
          desc.style.opacity = 0;
          desc.style.maxHeight = '0px';
        }

        // Title — inactive
        if (title) title.style.color = '#858f9f';

        // Reset progress instantly
        if (fill) {
          fill.style.transition = 'none';
          fill.style.height = '0%';
        }
      });

      // Active block 
      const activeBlock = blocks[index];
      activeBlock.classList.add('is-active');

      const desc = activeBlock.querySelector('.lounge-access_progress-decription');
      const title = activeBlock.querySelector('.lounge-access_progress-title');
      const fill = activeBlock.querySelector('.block-progress-fill');

      // Displaying the description smoothly (via CSS)
      if (desc) {
        desc.style.opacity = 1;
        desc.style.maxHeight = '300px';
      }

      if (title) title.style.color = '#fff';

      if (fill) {
        fill.style.transition = 'height 6s ease';
        fill.style.height = '100%';
      }
    }

    function nextBlock() {
      current = (current + 1) % blocks.length;
      activateBlock(current);
    }

    function startAutoCycle() {
      interval = setInterval(() => {
        nextBlock();
      }, 6000);
    }

    blocks.forEach((block, index) => {
      block.addEventListener('click', () => {
        clearInterval(interval);
        current = index;
        activateBlock(index);
        startAutoCycle();
      });
    });

    // Start
    activateBlock(current);
    startAutoCycle();
  });
</script></div><div class="lounge-access_content-column"><div data-index="0" class="lounge-access_block is-active"><div class="block-progress-line"><div class="block-progress-fill"></div></div><p class="lounge-access_progress-title">Pitchside Lounge</p><div class="spacer-xxsmall"></div><p class="lounge-access_progress-decription">Step into a realm where luxury hospitality and thrilling on-field action converge.   var Webflow = Webflow || [];
  Webflow.push(function () {
    const form = document.querySelector('[fifa="interest-form"]');
    if (!form) {
      console.error('❌ Form not found: [fifa="interest-form"]');
      return;
    }

    // ✅ Prevent browser from running native validation
    form.setAttribute("novalidate", "");

    // Decide endpoint based on origin
    const validOrigins = [
      "https://fifaworldcup26.hospitality.fifa.com",
      "https://webflow-fwc26.fifaworldcup26.onlocationexp.com",
    ];

    const apiUrl = validOrigins.includes(window.location.origin)
      ? "https://fifaworldcup26.hospitality.fifa.com/api/sfmc/submit-form"
      : "https://fifaworldcup26.pp-hospitality.fifa.com/api/sfmc/submit-form";

    // Helpers
    const getVal = (sel) => {
      const el = document.querySelector(sel);
      return el ? (el.value ?? "").trim() : "";
    };
    const getChecked = (sel) => {
      const el = document.querySelector(sel);
      return el ? !!el.checked : false;
    };

    // ✅ Check if element is visible
    const isVisible = (el) => {
      if (!el) return false;
      const style = window.getComputedStyle(el);
      if (style.display === "none" || style.visibility === "hidden") return false;
      const rect = el.getBoundingClientRect();
      return rect.width > 0 && rect.height > 0;
    };

    // ✅ Temporarily disable hidden required controls
    const disableHiddenRequired = () => {
      const toggled = [];
      form.querySelectorAll("input, select, textarea").forEach((el) => {
        if (el.required && !isVisible(el)) {
          toggled.push(el);
          el.disabled = true;
        }
      });
      return toggled;
    };

    // ✅ Restore controls after submit
    const restoreDisabled = (toggled) => {
      toggled.forEach((el) => (el.disabled = false));
    };

    // ✅ Get checked countries
    const getCheckedCountries = () => {
      const wrap = document.querySelector('[fifa="support-countries"]');
      if (!wrap) return [];
      return Array.from(wrap.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]:checked'))
        .map((el) => el.name || el.value || "")
        .filter(Boolean);
    };

    const getInterestedVenues = () => {
      const wrap = document.querySelector('[fifa="interested-venues"]');
      if (!wrap) return [];
      return Array.from(wrap.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]:checked'))
        .map((el) => el.name || el.value || "")
        .filter(Boolean);
    };

    // Venue multiselect update
    const venueWrapper = document.querySelector('[fifa="interested-venues"]');
    if (venueWrapper) {
      const venueCheckboxes = venueWrapper.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]');
      const venueLabel = document.querySelector("#venueLabel");
      venueCheckboxes.forEach((cb) => {
        cb.addEventListener("change", () => {
          if (venueLabel) venueLabel.textContent = getInterestedVenues().join(", ") || "Choose";
        });
      });
    }

    // Country multiselect update
    const countryWrapper = document.querySelector('[fifa="support-countries"]');
    if (countryWrapper) {
      const countryCheckboxes = countryWrapper.querySelectorAll('input[type="checkbox"]');
      const countryLabel = document.querySelector("#countryLabel");
      countryCheckboxes.forEach((cb) => {
        cb.addEventListener("change", () => {
          if (countryLabel) countryLabel.textContent = getCheckedCountries().join(", ") || "Choose";
        });
      });
    }

    // ✅ Helper to get UTM (sessionStorage first, then URL)
    const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
    const getUTM = (key) => {
      return (
        sessionStorage.getItem(key) || // prefer sessionStorage
        urlParams.get(key) || // fallback to URL
        ""
      );
    };

    // ✅ Detect preferred language
    const getPreferredLanguage = () => {
      const path = window.location.pathname;
      if (path.includes("/es/")) return "es-ES";
      if (path.includes("/fr/")) return "fr-FR";
      return "en-GB"; // default
    };

    form.addEventListener("submit", function (e) {
      e.preventDefault();

      // 🔒 Disable hidden required controls so browser doesn’t throw errors
      const toggled = disableHiddenRequired();

      const data = {
        // Step 1
        Multi_Form_First_Name: getVal('[name="Multi-Form-First-Name"]'),
        Multi_Form_Last_Name: getVal('[name="Multi-Form-Last-Name"]'),
        Multi_Form_Email: getVal('[name="Multi-Form-Email"]'),
        Multi_Form_Phone: getVal('[name="Multi-Form-Phone"]'),
        Multi_Form_Country: getVal('[name="Multi-Form-Country"]'),
        Multi_Form_State: getVal('[name="Multi-Form-State"]'),
        Multi_Form_Zip_Postal_Code: getVal('[name="Multi-Form-Zip-Postal-Code"]'),
        By_submitting_your_details_you_hereby_agree_to_receive_communications_from_FIFA_or_FIFA_Hospitality_Partners_about_FIFA_World_Cup_26_Official_Hospitality:
          getChecked(
            '[name="By-submitting-your-details-you-hereby-agree-to-receive-communications-from-FIFA-or-FIFA-Hospitality-Partners-about-FIFA-World-Cup-26-Official-Hospitality"]'
          ),

        // Step 2
        Private_Suite: getChecked('[name="Private-Suite"]'),
        Multi_Match_8_matches: getChecked('[name="Multi_Match_8_matches"]'),
        Multi_Match_2_4_matches: getChecked('[name="Multi_Match_2_4_matches"]'),
        Follow_My_Team_Series: getChecked('[name="Follow_My_Team_Series"]'),
        Venue_Series: getChecked('[name="Venue_Series"]'),
        Single_Match: getChecked('[name="Single_Match"]'),

        // Step 3
        Multi_Form_Purchase: getVal('[name="Multi-Form-Purchase"]'),
        Multi_Form_Group_Size: getVal('[name="Multi-Form-Group-Size"]'),
        Multi_Form_Budget_Range:
          getVal('[name="Multi-Form-Budget-Range-Group"]') || getVal('[name="Multi-Form-Budget-Range"]'),

        // Step 4
        Multi_Form_Company_Name: getVal('[name="Multi-Form-Company-Name"]'),
        Multi_Form_Company_Size: getVal('[name="Multi-Form-Company-Size"]'),
        Multi_Form_Company_Industry: getVal('[name="Multi-Form-Company-Industry"]'),
        Multi_Form_Company_Functional_Area: getVal('[name="Multi-Form-Company-Functional-Area"]'),

        // Step 5
        Multi_Form_Interested_Venue: getInterestedVenues().join(","),
        Multi_Form_Country_Support: getCheckedCountries().join(","),
        Multi_Form_Late_Rounds_Platinum: getVal('[name="Multi_Form_Late_Rounds_Platinum"]'),
        Multi_Form_Platinum_Access: getVal('[name="Multi-Form-Platinum-Access"]'),

        // Step 6
        Multi_Form_Shared: getVal('[name="Multi-Form-Shared"]'),
        Multi_Form_Venue: getVal('[name="Multi_Form_Venue"]'),
        Multi_Form_MLS: getVal('[name="Multi_Form_MLS"]'),
        Multi_Form_NFL: getVal('[name="Multi_Form_NFL"]'),
        Multi_Form_Travel: getVal('[name="Multi_Form_Travel"]'),
        Multi_Form_Social_Media: getVal('[name="Multi-Form-Social-Media"]'),
        Multi_Form_First_Hear: getVal('[name="Multi-Form-First-Hear"]'),

        // Step 7
        Multi_Form_Gender: getVal('[name="Multi-Form-Gender"]'),
        Multi_Form_Day_of_Birth: getVal('[name="Multi-Form-Day-of-Birth"]'),
        Multi_Form_Month_of_Birth: getVal('[name="Multi-Form-Month-of-Birth"]'),
        Multi_Form_Year_of_Birth: getVal('[name="Multi-Form-Year-of-Birth"]'),
        Multi_Form_Contact_Method: getVal('[name="Multi-Form-Contact-Method"]'),
        Multi_Form_Corp_Referral_Local_Fifa: window.location.pathname.includes("founderscard") ? "FoundersCard" : "",
        Receive_updates: getChecked('[name="Receive-updates"]'),
        Partner_Opt_In: getChecked('[name="Partner_Opt_In"]'),

        Preferred_Language: getPreferredLanguage(),

        Accommodation_Needed: getVal('[name="Multi-Form-Platinum-Access"]') === "Yes",

        // ✅ Pull UTM params from sessionStorage first
        utm_campaign: getUTM("utm_campaign"),
        utm_content: getUTM("utm_content"),
        utm_medium: getUTM("utm_medium"),
        utm_source: getUTM("utm_source"),
        utm_term: getUTM("utm_term"),
      };

      fetch(apiUrl, {
        method: "POST",
        headers: {
          accept: "application/json",
          "content-type": "application/json;charset=UTF-8",
        },
        body: JSON.stringify(data),
      })
        .then((res) => {
          if (!res.ok) throw new Error("Network response was not ok (" + res.status + ")");
          return res.json();
        })
        .then((json) => {
          console.log("✅ Success:", json);
          const done = form.parentElement?.querySelector(".w-form-done");
          const fail = form.parentElement?.querySelector(".w-form-fail");
          if (done) {
            form.style.display = "none";
            if (fail) fail.style.display = "none";
            done.style.display = "block";
          } else {
            alert("Form submitted successfully!");
          }
          form.reset();
        })
        .catch((err) => {
          console.error("❌ Submit error:", err);
          const fail = form.parentElement?.querySelector(".w-form-fail");
          if (fail) {
            fail.style.display = "block";
          } else {
            alert("There was a problem submitting the form.");
          }
        })
        .finally(() => {
          // 🔓 Restore controls
          restoreDisabled(toggled);
        });
    });
  });

document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
  const form = document.querySelector("form");
  const countrySelect = document.getElementById("Country");
  const countryCodeSelect = document.getElementById("Country");
  const phoneInput = document.getElementById("Phone");

  if (!countryCodeSelect || !phoneInput || !form) return;

  const TOP_COUNTRIES = ["US", "CA", "MX"];

  // 🔒 Phone disabled by default
  phoneInput.disabled = false;

  // ---------- helpers ----------

  function resetPhone() {
    phoneInput.value = "";
    phoneInput.dataset.local = "";
  }

  function getSelectedISO() {
    return countryCodeSelect.selectedOptions[0]?.value || null;
  }

  function applyLengthRule(iso) {
    const max = PHONE_LENGTH_BY_COUNTRY[iso];
    if (max) phoneInput.setAttribute("maxlength", max);
    else phoneInput.removeAttribute("maxlength");
  }

  // ---------- populate Country code select ----------

  function populateCountryCodeSelect() {
    countryCodeSelect.innerHTML = `<option value="" selected></option>`;

    // TOP countries first
    TOP_COUNTRIES.forEach(iso => {
      const country = COUNTRY_STATES.find(c => c.code === iso);
      const dial = COUNTRY_DIAL_CODES[iso];
      if (!country || !dial) return;

      const option = document.createElement("option");
      option.value = iso;
      option.dataset.dial = dial;
      option.textContent = `${country.name} (${dial})`;
      countryCodeSelect.appendChild(option);
    });

    // divider
    const divider = document.createElement("option");
    divider.disabled = true;
    divider.textContent = "──────────";
    countryCodeSelect.appendChild(divider);

    // rest alphabetically
    COUNTRY_STATES
      .filter(c => !TOP_COUNTRIES.includes(c.code))
      .sort((a, b) => a.name.localeCompare(b.name))
      .forEach(country => {
        const dial = COUNTRY_DIAL_CODES[country.code];
        if (!dial) return;

        const option = document.createElement("option");
        option.value = country.code;
        option.dataset.dial = dial;
        option.textContent = `${country.name} (${dial})`;
        countryCodeSelect.appendChild(option);
      });
  }

  // ---------- Country code change ----------

  countryCodeSelect.addEventListener("change", () => {
    const iso = getSelectedISO();
    if (!iso) return;

    resetPhone();
    applyLengthRule(iso);
    phoneInput.disabled = false;
    phoneInput.focus();
  });

  // ---------- Phone input (UI = local only) ----------

  phoneInput.addEventListener("input", () => {
    let digits = phoneInput.value.replace(/\D/g, "");

    const iso = getSelectedISO();
    const max = PHONE_LENGTH_BY_COUNTRY[iso];
    if (max && digits.length > max) {
      digits = digits.slice(0, max);
    }

    phoneInput.value = digits;        
    phoneInput.dataset.local = digits;  
  });

  // ---------- BEFORE SUBMIT → inject full phone for CRM ----------

  form.addEventListener("submit", () => {
    const selected = countryCodeSelect.selectedOptions[0];
    const local = phoneInput.dataset.local || "";

    if (!selected || !local) return;

    const dial = selected.dataset.dial;
    phoneInput.value = dial + local; 
  });
});
</script></div></div></div><section id="about" class="padding-global"><div class="section-space-xlarge"></div><div class="container-medium"><div class="simple-horizontal-block"><div <script>(()=>{var t="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/@finsweet/attributes-accordion@1/accordion.js",e=document.querySelector(`script[src="${t}"]`);e||(e=document.createElement("script"),e.async=!0,e.src=t,document.head.append(e));})();</script>
<!-- LOCAL: Run code after FS Attributes 
<script src="http://127.0.0.1:5500/_code/accordion.js"></script>

<!-- Run code after FS Attributes -->
<script>
// Define a unique key to store the initialization flag on the window object
const ACCORDION_INIT_FLAG = 'finsweetAccordionInitialized'

// Check if the script has already been initialized
if (window[ACCORDION_INIT_FLAG]) {
    console.warn('Finsweet Accordion script has already been initialized.')
} else {
    // Function to initialize accordions
    function initializeAccordions() {
        // Select all accordion groups
        const accordionGroups = document.querySelectorAll(
            '[fs-accordion-element="group"]'
        )

        // Select rich text to clone accordions from, if it exists
        const richtextElement = document.querySelector(
            '[data-accordion-element="richtext"]'
        )

        // Select a template accordion to clone
        const templateAccordion = document.querySelector(
            '[fs-accordion-element="accordion"]'
        )

        // If no groups, richtext, or template accordion found, exit the script
        if (
            accordionGroups.length === 0 &&
            !richtextElement &&
            !templateAccordion
        ) {
            console.info(
                'No accordion groups, rich text element, or template accordion found. Finsweet Accordion script will not run.'
            )
            return
        }

        // Utility function to generate a readable unique ID
        function generateReadableId(index, type, groupIndex) {
            return `accordion-${groupIndex + 1}-${type}-${index + 1}`
        }

        // Function to create accordions from richtext headings and paragraphs
        function createAccordionsFromRichText() {
            if (!richtextElement || !templateAccordion) return

            // Find all headings (questions) and the following paragraphs (answers)
            const headings = richtextElement.querySelectorAll('h3, h2, h4')
            const accordionContainer = templateAccordion.parentElement

            headings.forEach((heading, index) => {
                const nextElement = heading.nextElementSibling

                if (
                    nextElement &&
                    (nextElement.tagName === 'P' ||
                        nextElement.tagName === 'DIV')
                ) {
                    if (index === 0) {
                        // Use the original accordion as the first accordion for the rich text
                        const label = templateAccordion.querySelector(
                            '[data-accordion-element="label"]'
                        )
                        const content = templateAccordion.querySelector(
                            '[data-accordion-element="content"]'
                        )

                        label.textContent = heading.textContent
                        content.innerHTML = nextElement.outerHTML

                        // Assign a unique ID to the trigger and content of the original accordion
                        const trigger = templateAccordion.querySelector(
                            '[fs-accordion-element="trigger"]'
                        )
                        const triggerId = generateReadableId(index, 'header', 0)
                        const contentId = generateReadableId(
                            index,
                            'content',
                            0
                        )

                        trigger.id = triggerId
                        content.id = contentId
                        trigger.setAttribute('aria-controls', content.id)
                        content.setAttribute('aria-labelledby', trigger.id)
                    } else {
                        // Clone the template accordion for subsequent rich text items
                        const accordion = templateAccordion.cloneNode(true)

                        // Find the label and content elements in the cloned accordion
                        const label = accordion.querySelector(
                            '[data-accordion-element="label"]'
                        )
                        const content = accordion.querySelector(
                            '[data-accordion-element="content"]'
                        )

                        // Update the label and content with the new question and answer
                        label.textContent = heading.textContent
                        content.innerHTML = nextElement.outerHTML

                        // Assign a unique ID to the trigger and content
                        const trigger = accordion.querySelector(
                            '[fs-accordion-element="trigger"]'
                        )
                        const triggerId = generateReadableId(index, 'header', 0)
                        const contentId = generateReadableId(
                            index,
                            'content',
                            0
                        )

                        trigger.id = triggerId
                        content.id = contentId
                        trigger.setAttribute('aria-controls', content.id)
                        content.setAttribute('aria-labelledby', trigger.id)

                        // Append the cloned accordion to the container
                        accordionContainer.appendChild(accordion)
                    }
                }
            })
        }

        // Function to scroll to the start of the group + heights of previous accordion triggers
        function scrollToAccordionTrigger(group, clickedTrigger) {
            const groupTop =
                group.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.pageYOffset
            const allTriggers = group.querySelectorAll(
                '[fs-accordion-element="trigger"]'
            )
            let totalHeight = 0

            for (let i = 0; i < allTriggers.length; i++) {
                const trigger = allTriggers[i]
                if (trigger === clickedTrigger) break

                const triggerHeight = trigger.getBoundingClientRect().height
                const triggerStyle = window.getComputedStyle(trigger)
                const marginBottom = parseFloat(triggerStyle.marginBottom)
                totalHeight += triggerHeight + marginBottom
            }

            const scrollPosition = groupTop + totalHeight
            window.scrollTo({ top: scrollPosition, behavior: 'smooth' })
        }

        // Initialize rich text based accordions
        createAccordionsFromRichText()

        // Initialize existing accordion groups if any
        accordionGroups.forEach((group, groupIndex) => {
            const interactionType = group.getAttribute(
                'fs-accordion-interaction'
            )
            const accordions = group.querySelectorAll(
                '[fs-accordion-element="accordion"]'
            )

            accordions.forEach((accordion, index) => {
                const trigger = accordion.querySelector(
                    '[fs-accordion-element="trigger"]'
                )
                const content = accordion.querySelector(
                    '[fs-accordion-element="content"]'
                )

                if (trigger && content) {
                    const triggerId = generateReadableId(
                        index,
                        'header',
                        groupIndex
                    )
                    const contentId = generateReadableId(
                        index,
                        'content',
                        groupIndex
                    )

                    trigger.id = triggerId
                    content.id = contentId
                    trigger.setAttribute('aria-controls', content.id)
                    content.setAttribute('aria-labelledby', trigger.id)

                    if (interactionType === 'one') {
                        trigger.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
                            const isExpanded =
                                trigger.getAttribute('aria-expanded') === 'true'
                            scrollToAccordionTrigger(group, trigger)
                            if (isExpanded) return

                            setTimeout(function () {
                                const updatedAccordions =
                                    group.querySelectorAll(
                                        '[fs-accordion-element="accordion"]'
                                    )
                                updatedAccordions.forEach((otherAccordion) => {
                                    const otherTrigger =
                                        otherAccordion.querySelector(
                                            '[fs-accordion-element="trigger"]'
                                        )
                                    if (
                                        otherTrigger !== trigger &&
                                        otherTrigger.getAttribute(
                                            'aria-expanded'
                                        ) === 'true'
                                    ) {
                                        otherTrigger.click()
                                    }
                                })
                            }, 10)
                        })
                    } else if (interactionType === 'multiple') {
                        trigger.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
                            scrollToAccordionTrigger(group, trigger)
                        })
                    }
                } else {
                    console.warn(
                        'Accordion is missing either a trigger or content element:',
                        accordion
                    )
                }
            })
        })

        window[ACCORDION_INIT_FLAG] = true
        console.log('Finsweet Accordion attributes have been successfully set.')
    }

    if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
            initializeAccordions()
        })
    } else {
        initializeAccordions()
    }
}
</script></div><div class="faqschema_script w-embed w-script"><!-- Enhanced FAQ Schema Script with Window Global Storage -->
<script>
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
        // Function to generate or extend the FAQ Schema
        function generateFAQSchema() {
            // Check if the FAQ schema is already stored in the window object
            if (!window.faqSchema) {
                window.faqSchema = {
                    "@context": "https://schema.org",
                    "@type": "FAQPage",
                    "mainEntity": []
                };
            }

            const faqSchema = window.faqSchema;

            // Helper function to check if a question already exists
            function isDuplicateQuestion(question) {
                return faqSchema.mainEntity.some(item => item.name === question);
            }

            // Function to add question and answer to schema if both are not empty
            function addToSchema(question, answer) {
                if (question && answer && !isDuplicateQuestion(question)) {
                    faqSchema.mainEntity.push({
                        "@type": "Question",
                        "name": question,
                        "acceptedAnswer": {
                            "@type": "Answer",
                            "text": answer
                        }
                    });
                }
            }

            const accordions = document.querySelectorAll('.accordion_component[data-accordion]');
            accordions.forEach(acc => {
                const questionEl = acc.querySelector('[data-accordion-element="label"]');
                const answerContainer = acc.querySelector('[data-accordion-element="content"]');
                const answerEl = answerContainer?.querySelector('p');
                const questionText = questionEl?.textContent?.trim();
                const answerText = answerEl?.textContent?.trim();
                addToSchema(questionText, answerText);
            });

            // Check if schema exists in the document head
            if (!document.querySelector('script[type="application/ld+json"][data-schema="faq"]')) {
                // Convert the schema object to a JSON-LD script tag if schema has entries
                if (faqSchema.mainEntity.length > 0) {
                    const script = document.createElement('script');
                    script.type = 'application/ld+json';
                    script.setAttribute('data-schema', 'faq'); // Mark this as our FAQ schema
                    script.textContent = JSON.stringify(faqSchema, null, 2);
                    document.head.appendChild(script);
                }
            }
        }

        // Call the function to generate or extend the FAQ schema
        generateFAQSchema();
    });

  const lstCountries = ['us', 'ca', 'mx'];
  const lstLanguages = ['en', 'es', 'fr'];

  const addSubroutes = (mainRoute, subRoutes, inverted = false) => {
    const lstRoutes = [];
    subRoutes.forEach((subRoute) => {
      if (inverted) {
        lstRoutes.push(`${subRoute}/${mainRoute}`);
      } else {
        lstRoutes.push(`${mainRoute}/${subRoute}`);
      }
    });
    return lstRoutes;
  };

  const validSubRoutes = new Set(['', ...addSubroutes('us', lstLanguages), ...addSubroutes('mx', lstLanguages), ...addSubroutes('ca', lstLanguages), 'faq', ...addSubroutes('faq', lstLanguages, true), 'hospitalitysupport', ...addSubroutes('hospitalitysupport', lstLanguages, true)]);

  const currentSubPathIsValid = () => {
    const subPath = globalThis.location.pathname.replaceAll(/(^\/+)|(\/+$)/g, '');
    return validSubRoutes.has(subPath);
  };

  const getLangFromHtmlAttribute = () => {
    const htmlLang = (document.documentElement?.getAttribute('lang') || '').toLowerCase();

    if (htmlLang.startsWith('es')) {
      return 'es';
    }

    if (htmlLang.startsWith('fr')) {
      return 'fr';
    }

    return 'en';
  };

  const injectIphoneChatCssFix = () => {
    const styleId = 'embeddedMessagingFrameIphoneFix';
    const styleTag = document.createElement('style');
    styleTag.id = styleId;
    styleTag.textContent = '#embeddedMessagingFrame { max-height: calc(100dvh - 9em) !important; }';
    document.head.appendChild(styleTag);
  };

  const environments = {
    uat: {
      orgId: '00DV9000006H5fl',
      deploymentName: 'Agentforce_Iris',
      baseUrl: 'https://onlocationexp--agentuat.sandbox.my.site.com/ESWAgentforceIris1778055798781',
      scrt2URL: 'https://onlocationexp--agentuat.sandbox.my.salesforce-scrt.com',
    },
    prod: {
      orgId: '00D50000000byzq',
      deploymentName: 'Agentforce_Iris',
      baseUrl: 'https://onlocationexp.my.site.com/ESWAgentforceIris1778055798781',
      scrt2URL: 'https://onlocationexp.my.salesforce-scrt.com',
    },
  };

  const getCurrentEnv = () => {
    return globalThis.origin == 'https://fifaworldcup26.hospitality.fifa.com' ? 'prod' : 'uat';
  };

  function loadEmbeddedMessagingScript() {
    if (!currentSubPathIsValid()) {
      return;
    }

    const config = environments[getCurrentEnv()];
    const bootstrapScript = document.createElement('script');
    bootstrapScript.type = 'text/javascript';
    bootstrapScript.src = `${config.baseUrl}/assets/js/bootstrap.min.js`;
    bootstrapScript.onload = () => {
      injectIphoneChatCssFix();
      initEmbeddedMessaging(config);
      console.log('Salesforce chat script loaded successfully from: ', bootstrapScript.src);
    };
    bootstrapScript.onerror = () => {
      console.error('Error loading Salesforce bootstrap script from: ', bootstrapScript.src);
    };
    document.head.appendChild(bootstrapScript);
  }

  let lang = getLangFromHtmlAttribute();
  function initEmbeddedMessaging(config) {
    try {
      embeddedservice_bootstrap.settings.language = lang;
      embeddedservice_bootstrap.init(config.orgId, config.deploymentName, config.baseUrl, {
        scrt2URL: config.scrt2URL,
      });

      globalThis.addEventListener('onEmbeddedMessagingReady', () => {
        embeddedservice_bootstrap.prechatAPI.setHiddenPrechatFields({
          EndUserLanguage: embeddedservice_bootstrap.settings.language,
        });
      });
    } catch (err) {
      console.error('Error loading Embedded Messaging: ', err);
    }
  }

  loadEmbeddedMessagingScript();
